# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Research question:

- How can interaction with non-human agents
    inform our relationship digital systems?
- How does the presence of a non-human agent 
    affect our experience qualitatively? 
 ^2SyI2S6k

early digital systems
neural representation
emergence of new media ^s0XwXNj1

diff uses of ML
user/viewer experience
format/concept for installation ^xC0gIZuG

TD Neuron
Preempting motion  ^RSJfuJeN

III. ML Training
- Using program TD Neuron which will be trained live by participant interaction
 ^2wGVITis

IV. Installation
- Large room to facilitate movement
- Visible cameras for video stream
 ^D5OOeFC3

The paper will contain:
- An introduction on cybernetics: 
    - Historical background on the early metaphorical descriptions of ANNs and the 
        interdisciplinary thought that led to the creation of NNs as we know them
        - Macy Conferences, "How We Became Posthuman"
- An introduction on digital art: 
    - An overview of how artists began to represent digital relationships; 
        visualizations of the digital, Nam June Paik, etc. 
- Specific examples of ANNs/ML in contemporary art
    - Amber Frid-Jimenez: use of ML to interpret static data input
    - Marco Barotti: use of ML to visualize (& create sound from) live data input
- Why is this valuable to cognitive science?
    - A philosophical analysis of the value of images and how metaphor shapes 
    our understanding of AI 
    - Embodiment? ^Qoray3nY

The paper serves to contextualize and support the installation as a work in the field of cognitive science.  ^EcLaOGbA

The role of visual metaphor in understanding and relating to artificial agents ^1ZJUYNw5

Methodology for the installation: 

I. Visuals 

II. Training ML model in TD Neuron

III. Installation space, beta-testing

IV. Final installation ^wlzB8HAZ

The project will culminate in a research paper and an installation ^KLYCVJYV

Dual Methodology ^bKBvTje9

Expected results, big picture  ^sThlWL6h
